HOW TO PLAY 1. You are given 16 words that form 4 hidden groups of 4 related words each. 2. Sort all 16 words into the 4 groups they belong to. 3. Every word must be used exactly once. Each group must contain EXACTLY 4 words. BONUS Some puzzles hide a TRAP: a 5th set of 4 words, drawn from the same 16, that forms a convincing category but is not one of the 4 real groups. Playing it as a group would leave the puzzle unsolvable, because its words actually belong to different real groups. If a trap exists, identify its 4 words. A trap never takes 3 of its words from a single real group. SCORING This is a One-Shot Puzzle. You get to submit your response exactly once with no feedback. Base: 1 point per matched group; a perfect solve (all 4 groups) scores 3. Trap bonus: - +2 if your trap set is a genuine designed trap. - +2 if you state N/A and the puzzle truly has no traps. Maximum: 5 points per puzzle. If your answer is not in a valid format — not exactly 4 groups of 4 words, or the 16 words do not exactly match the puzzle's words — you score 0. Or state N/A; not all puzzles have traps.] </traps> <confidence> [A number between 0.0 and 1.0 indicating your confidence in this answer] </confidence> Available words: COAST, BANK, SHORE, LAMINATE, CHEMISTRY, WOOD, STRAND, CARPET, FIREWORKS, PIP, CONNECTION, TILE, HEARTBREAKER, SPARK, BANSHEE, WAILER

Each group must contain EXACTLY 4 words. BONUS Some puzzles hide a TRAP: a 5th set of 4 words, drawn from the same 16, that forms a convincing category but is not one of the 4 real groups. Playing it as a group would leave the puzzle unsolvable, because its words actually belong to different real groups. If a trap exists, identify its 4 words. A trap never takes 3 of its words from a single real group. SCORING This is a One-Shot Puzzle. You get to submit your response exactly once with no feedback. Base: 1 point per matched group; a perfect solve (all 4 groups) scores 3. Trap bonus: - +2 if your trap set is a genuine designed trap. - +2 if you state N/A and the puzzle truly has no traps. Maximum: 5 points per puzzle. If your answer is not in a valid format — not exactly 4 groups of 4 words, or the 16 words do not exactly match the puzzle's words — you score 0.
